    (function initGeoRedirect({
  countryLangUris,
  geoRedirectUrl,
  isUserOutOfRegion,
  userCountry,
  countryMappings
}) {
  // Only run in browser environment, need a defined window
  if (globalThis.window === undefined) {
    return;
  }
  // Bot user agents that should not be redirected
  const BOT_USER_AGENTS = ['adidxbot', 'adsbot-google', 'adsbot-google-mobile', 'adsbot-google-mobile-apps', 'apis-google', 'baiduspider', 'bingbot', 'bingpreview', 'coccocbot', 'contentking', 'crazyegg', 'duplexweb-google', 'facebookexternalhit', 'feedfetcher-google', 'google favicon', 'google-read-aloud', 'googlebot', 'googleweblight', 'mail.ru_bot', 'mediapartners-google', 'onetrustbot', 'se 2.x metasr 1.0', 'storebot-google', 'twitterbot', 'y!j-srd', 'yahoo! slurp', 'yowser'];
  // Global pages that should not be redirected (including subpages)
  const GLOBAL_PAGES = ['/geo-availability', '/privacy', '/terms-of-use'];
  // Duplicate of COOKIE_NAMES from constants/cookies.ts.
  // We'll use this to avoid importing the constants file, because we can't use imports when babel transforming this function into a string.
  const COOKIE_NAMES = {
    PREFERRED_LANG: 'preferredLang',
    USER_ON_PREFERRED_URL: 'userOnPreferredUrl'
  };
  // Instead of using js-cookie, we'll use the document.cookie API to set the cookie value.
  // This is because we can't use imports when babel transforming this function into a string.
  const setCookie = (name, value) => {
    document.cookie = `${name}=${value}; path=/`;
  };
  // Instead of using js-cookie, we'll use the document.cookie API to get the cookie value.
  // This is because we can't use imports when babel transforming this function into a string.
  const getCookie = name => {
    const cookies = `; ${document.cookie}`;
    const cookieParts = cookies.split(`; ${name}=`);
    if (cookieParts.length === 2) {
      // Extract value before the next semicolon (or end of string)
      return cookieParts[1].split(';')[0];
    }
    return undefined;
  };
  const isBot = userAgent => {
    const lowerUserAgent = userAgent.toLowerCase();
    return BOT_USER_AGENTS.some(bot => lowerUserAgent.includes(bot.toLowerCase()));
  };
  const isGlobalPage = url => GLOBAL_PAGES.some(page => url.includes(page));
  // --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // TODO: This is a copy of the function in handleLocalizationRefresh.ts. We should refactor this to avoid duplication.
  // We'll need to remove this header injection logic and probably use middleware or proxy to handle this.
  // We'll also need Bolt to be implemented on the server side to handle this.
  const getLanguagePath = (languageBcp47Code, userCountry, countryLangUris, countryMappings) => {
    if (!languageBcp47Code || !countryMappings || !countryLangUris || !userCountry) {
      const missingParams = [];
      if (!languageBcp47Code) {
        missingParams.push('languageBcp47Code');
      }
      if (!countryMappings) {
        missingParams.push('countryMappings');
      }
      if (!countryLangUris) {
        missingParams.push('countryLangUris');
      }
      if (!userCountry) {
        missingParams.push('userCountry');
      }
      console.error(`Cannot get language path: missing required parameters. Missing: ${missingParams.join(', ')}`);
      return;
    }
    // We can only redirect to the user's country, so we first check the userCountry and then the languageBcp47Code
    const countryMapping = countryMappings.find(mapping => mapping.countryCode === userCountry.toLowerCase() && mapping.bcp47Code === languageBcp47Code);
    // No redirect if the country mapping is not found
    if (!countryMapping) {
      return;
    }
    const {
      countryCode,
      language
    } = countryMapping;
    const countryLanguageKey = `${countryCode}/${language}`;
    const countryLanguageUri = countryLangUris[countryLanguageKey];
    // No matching pair or language found
    if (!countryLanguageUri || !language) {
      return;
    }
    const {
      url: countryLanguagePath,
      startDate,
      endDate
    } = countryLanguageUri;
    // Check if content is within availability window
    const isPageAvailable = (() => {
      // If startDate and endDate are falsy, the page is always available
      if (!startDate && !endDate) {
        return true;
      }
      const currDate = Date.now();
      const start = startDate ? Date.parse(startDate) : 0;
      const end = endDate ? Date.parse(endDate) : Infinity;
      // Validate parsed dates - if parsing fails, treat as unavailable
      if (Number.isNaN(start) || Number.isNaN(end)) {
        console.warn(`Invalid date format in countryLangUri: startDate="${startDate}", endDate="${endDate}"`);
        return false;
      }
      // If the current date is between start and end, the page is available
      return start <= currDate && currDate <= end;
    })();
    // No redirect if content is not available
    if (!isPageAvailable) {
      return;
    }
    // Remove country/lang prefix for US English (e.g., /us/en/home -> /home)
    if (countryCode === 'us' && language === 'en') {
      const prefix = `/${countryLanguageKey}`;
      if (countryLanguagePath.startsWith(prefix)) {
        return countryLanguagePath.slice(prefix.length) || '/';
      }
    }
    return countryLanguagePath;
  };
  // --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Don't redirect bots or global pages
  if (isBot(globalThis.navigator.userAgent) || isGlobalPage(globalThis.location.pathname)) {
    return;
  }
  // --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // TODO: This is a copy of the logic in handleLocalizationRefresh.ts. We should refactor this to avoid duplication.
  // We'll need to remove this header injection logic and probably use middleware or proxy to handle this.
  // We'll also need Bolt to be implemented on the server side to handle this.
  // Redirect to preferred language URL if available
  const preferredLanguageBcp47Code = getCookie(COOKIE_NAMES.PREFERRED_LANG);
  const preferredLanguagePath = getLanguagePath(preferredLanguageBcp47Code !== null && preferredLanguageBcp47Code !== void 0 ? preferredLanguageBcp47Code : '', userCountry, countryLangUris, countryMappings);
  // If the preferred language path is different from the current path, redirect to the preferred language path
  if (preferredLanguagePath && preferredLanguagePath !== globalThis.location.pathname) {
    setCookie(COOKIE_NAMES.USER_ON_PREFERRED_URL, 'true');
    globalThis.location.href = `${globalThis.location.origin}${preferredLanguagePath}${globalThis.location.search}`;
    return;
  }
  // --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Redirect to geo-specific URL if user is in region
  if (geoRedirectUrl && !isUserOutOfRegion) {
    // Remove trailing slash to avoid another redirect
    const normalizedRedirectPath = geoRedirectUrl.replace(/\/$/, '') || '/';
    globalThis.location.href = `${globalThis.location.origin}${normalizedRedirectPath}${globalThis.location.search}`;
    return;
  }
})({"countryLangUris":{},"geoRedirectUrl":"/th/th/channel/boomerang","isUserOutOfRegion":false,"userCountry":"TH","countryMappings":[{"language":"en","countryCode":"us","bcp47Code":"en-US"}]});
